<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:виснуть.html>ви́снуть</a> (24940)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A primary verb in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:висеть.html>висе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">visétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:виснуть.html>ви́снуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vísnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to droop, to hang down, to dangle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang on <i>(to)</i>, to cling <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:виснуть.html>ви́снуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шея.html>ше́е</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vísnutʹ</b> u kovó-libo na šéje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hang on smb's neck</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to freeze up
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зависнуть.html>зави́снуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zavísnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:виснуть.html>ви́снущий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vísnuščij</span>)
</p>

***висок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:висок.html>висо́к</a> (4366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:висеть.html>висе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">visétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hang</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; original meaning (still found dialectally) "hair hanging at the temples". Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">виска́та</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">viskáta</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slovenly woman with disheveled hair</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:висок.html>висо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">visók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:висок.html>виска́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:висок.html>виски́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:висок.html>виско́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> temple</li></ol>

***витать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:витать.html>вита́ть</a> (11312)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vitati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dwell; to welcome</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:витать.html>вита́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vitátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to hover <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to float in the air</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to soar <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to fly aloft with little effort; to rise in thought, spirits, or imagination; to be exalted in mood</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:витать.html>вита́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:облако.html>облака́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vitátʹ</b> v oblakáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be head in the clouds</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dwell, to be present invisibly, to be in the air (of smell, of sensation, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dwell, to stay somewhere</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to greet</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вита́ние</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vitánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:витать.html>вита́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:облако.html>облака́х</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vitátʹ v oblakáx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***вить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a> (30532)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">viti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vī́tī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weh₁y-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свить.html>свить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wind</li>
<li>to twist, to weave
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:венок.html>вено́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vitʹ</b> venók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to weave a garland</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнездо.html>гнездо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vitʹ</b> gnezdó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to build / make a nest; <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to put down roots in some place, to settle down in some place</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:веревка.html>верёвки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> кого́-либо</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vitʹ</b> verjóvki iz kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn / twist smb. round one's little finger</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***виться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:виться.html>ви́ться</a> (7767)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>ви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:виться.html>ви́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><i>(hair)</i> to wave, to curl</li>
<li><i>(plants)</i> to twine <i>(about, round)</i></li>
<li><i>(birds, insects etc.)</i> to hover</li>
<li><i>(sut etc.)</i> to eddy, to whirl</li>
<li><i>(river, road)</i> to wind, to meander</li>
<li><i>(snake)</i> to twist, to writhe</li>
<li>to flutter</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>ви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вихор.html>вихо́р</a> (21793)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вихор.html>вихо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vixór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вихор.html>вихра́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вихор.html>вихры́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вихор.html>вихро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tuft, forelock, cowlick</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***вихрь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вихрь.html>вихрь</a> (6624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вихърь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vixŭrĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vixъrъ</i>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вихрь.html>вихрь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vixrʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вихрь.html>ви́хря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вихрь.html>ви́хри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вихрь.html>ви́хрей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>whirlwind</li>
<li>vortex, swirl</li>
<li>eddy, twirl</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вишь.html>вишь</a> (11658)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вколо́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vkolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вкалывать.html>вка́лывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vkályvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вколо́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(in, into)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to inject <i>(to)</i>, to give a shot <i>(of)</i></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вкалывать.html>вка́лывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vkályvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work hard, to sweat <i>(one's guts out)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клад.html>клад</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klad</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">treasure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вклад.html>вклад</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vklad</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вклад.html>вкла́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вклад.html>вкла́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вклад.html>вкла́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deposit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">money placed in an account</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, account (<i>in a bank</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бессрочный.html>бессро́чный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вклад.html>вклад</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bessróčnyj <b>vklad</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">demand deposit, current account</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>contribution <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something given or offered that adds to a larger whole</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вклад.html>вклад</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наука.html>нау́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vnosítʹ bolʹšój <b>vklad</b> v naúku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make an important contribution to science</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вкладываться.html>вкла́дываться</a> (28837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вкладывать.html>вкла́дывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vkládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вкладываться.html>вкла́дываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vkládyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вложи́ться</b>)
</p>
